📄 FILE 20: application/services/project_manager.py
"""Project lifecycle manager with resume capability and interactive enhancement."""import asyncioimport jsonimport osfrom typing import Optional, Dict, List, Callablefrom datetime import datetimefrom pathlib import Pathimport structlogimport aiosqlitefrom domain.project_entities import Project, ProjectStatus, EnhancementProposal, Checkpointfrom infrastructure.llm.resilience import ResilientLLMClientfrom application.services.notification_service import NotificationService, Severitylogger = structlog.get_logger()class ProjectRepository:    """SQLite-backed project storage."""        def __init__(self, db_path: str = "data/projects.db"):        self.db_path = db_path        self._ensure_dir()        def _ensure_dir(self):        Path(self.db_path).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)        async def initialize(self):        """Create tables."""        async with aiosqlite.connect(self.db_path) as db:            await db.execute("""                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (                    project_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,                    user_id TEXT NOT NULL,                    data TEXT NOT NULL,                    status TEXT NOT NULL,                    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP                )            """)            await db.execute("""                CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_user_status                 ON projects(user_id, status)            """)            await db.commit()        async def save(self, project: Project):        """Persist project state."""        async with aiosqlite.connect(self.db_path) as db:            await db.execute("""                INSERT OR REPLACE INTO projects (project_id, user_id, data, status, updated_at)                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)            """, (                project.project_id,                project.user_id,                json.dumps(project.to_dict()),                project.status.name,                datetime.utcnow().isoformat()            ))            await db.commit()        logger.debug("project_saved", project_id=project.project_id, status=project.status.name)        async def load(self, project_id: str) -> Optional[Project]:        """Load project by ID."""        async with aiosqlite.connect(self.db_path) as db:            async with db.execute(                "SELECT data FROM projects WHERE project_id = ?", (project_id,)            ) as cursor:                row = await cursor.fetchone()                if row:                    return Project.from_dict(json.loads(row[0]))                return None        async def load_by_user(self, user_id: str, status: Optional[ProjectStatus] = None) -> List[Project]:        """Load user's projects, optionally filtered by status."""        async with aiosqlite.connect(self.db_path) as db:            if status:                cursor = await db.execute(                    "SELECT data FROM projects WHERE user_id = ? AND status = ? ORDER BY updated_at DESC",                    (user_id, status.name)                )            else:                cursor = await db.execute(                    "SELECT data FROM projects WHERE user_id = ? ORDER BY updated_at DESC",                    (user_id,)                )                        rows = await cursor.fetchall()            return [Project.from_dict(json.loads(r[0])) for r in rows]        async def get_resumable(self, user_id: str) -> List[Project]:        """Get projects that can be resumed."""        resumable_statuses = ["PAUSED", "FAILED", "CHECKPOINT"]        placeholders = ",".join(["?" for _ in resumable_statuses])                async with aiosqlite.connect(self.db_path) as db:            cursor = await db.execute(                f"SELECT data FROM projects WHERE user_id = ? AND status IN ({placeholders})",                (user_id, *resumable_statuses)            )            rows = await cursor.fetchall()            return [Project.from_dict(json.loads(r[0])) for r in rows]class EnhancementEngine:    """    Analyzes user requests and generates improvement proposals.    """        def __init__(self, llm_client: ResilientLLMClient):        self.llm = llm_client        async def analyze_and_propose(self, project: Project) -> List[EnhancementProposal]:        """        Generate enhancement proposals based on user request.        """        prompt = f"""        Analyze this task request and suggest 3-5 enhancements:                User Request: "{project.user_request}"                Categories to consider:        1. Scope: Missing requirements, edge cases, validation steps        2. Quality: Error handling, logging, documentation        3. Safety: Backup strategies, rollback plans, permissions        4. Efficiency: Parallelization, caching, algorithmic improvements                For each proposal, provide:        - Title (short)        - Description (what to add)        - Rationale (why it helps)        - Impact (low/medium/high)        - Estimated additional cost (if applicable)                Format as JSON list.        """                try:            response = await self.llm.complete(                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],                temperature=0.7            )                        # Parse proposals from LLM response            proposals_data = self._extract_proposals(response.content)            proposals = []                        for data in proposals_data:                proposals.append(EnhancementProposal(                    category=data.get("category", "general"),                    title=data["title"],                    description=data["description"],                    rationale=data["rationale"],                    impact_estimate=data.get("impact", "medium"),                    additional_cost_usd=self._estimate_cost(data.get("effort", "medium"))                ))                        return proposals                    except Exception as e:            logger.error("enhancement_analysis_failed", error=str(e))            return []        def _extract_proposals(self, content: str) -> List[Dict]:        """Extract structured proposals from LLM text."""        # Simple extraction - in production use structured JSON mode        import re        try:            # Look for JSON array            match = re.search(r'$$.*$$', content, re.DOTALL)            if match:                return json.loads(match.group())        except:            pass                # Fallback: parse bullet points        proposals = []        lines = content.split('\n')        current = {}                for line in lines:            if line.strip().startswith('- ') or line.strip().startswith('* '):                if current and 'title' in current:                    proposals.append(current)                current = {"title": line.strip('- *').split(':')[0]}            elif ':' in line and current:                key, val = line.split(':', 1)                current[key.lower().strip()] = val.strip()                if current:            proposals.append(current)                return proposals        def _estimate_cost(self, effort: str) -> Optional[float]:        """Rough cost estimation."""        costs = {"low": 0.05, "medium": 0.15, "high": 0.50}        return costs.get(effort.lower())class ProjectManager:    """    Main orchestrator for project lifecycle with resume capability.    """        def __init__(        self,        repository: ProjectRepository,        enhancement_engine: EnhancementEngine,        notification_service: NotificationService,        execution_callback: Optional[Callable] = None    ):        self.repo = repository        self.enhancer = enhancement_engine        self.notifier = notification_service        self.execute_task = execution_callback                # Active projects awaiting user input        self._awaiting_review: Dict[str, asyncio.Event] = {}        self._user_responses: Dict[str, str] = {}        async def initialize(self):        """Initialize repository."""        await self.repo.initialize()        async def create_project(        self,         user_id: str,         request: str,         channels: Dict[str, str]    ) -> Project:        """        Create new project and start enhancement analysis.        """        project = Project(            user_id=user_id,            user_request=request,            original_request=request,            notification_channels=channels        )                # Save initial state        await self.repo.save(project)                # Start async analysis        asyncio.create_task(self._analyze_project(project.project_id))                return project        async def _analyze_project(self, project_id: str):        """Background analysis and proposal generation."""        project = await self.repo.load(project_id)        if not project:            return                project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.ANALYZING, "Starting enhancement analysis")        await self.repo.save(project)                # Generate proposals        proposals = await self.enhancer.analyze_and_propose(project)        project.proposals = proposals                # Create enhanced description        approved_addons = [p for p in proposals if p.approved is not False]  # Default include unless rejected        enhancement_text = "\n".join([f"- {p.title}" for p in approved_addons])        project.enhanced_description = f"{project.original_request}\n\nEnhancements:\n{enhancement_text}"                project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.PROPOSED, "Enhancements ready for review")        await self.repo.save(project)                # Notify user        await self._notify_proposals_ready(project)        async def _notify_proposals_ready(self, project: Project):        """Send proposals to user via appropriate channel."""        message = f"""🎯 *New Project Created: {project.project_id}**Original Request:*_{project.original_request}_{project.get_proposal_summary()}*Estimated Cost:* ${project.estimated_cost_usd or 'TBD'}Reply to:• Toggle proposals (e.g., "approve 1,3" or "reject 2")• Add notes (e.g., "note: also handle edge case X")• "execute" to proceed with approved proposals• "cancel" to abort        """                # Send to all registered channels        for channel_type, channel_id in project.notification_channels.items():            if channel_type == "telegram":                await self.notifier.notify(                    severity=Severity.INFO,                    title=f"Project {project.project_id} Ready for Review",                    message=message,                    channels=["telegram"]                )            elif channel_type == "slack":                await self.notifier.notify(                    severity=Severity.INFO,                    title=f"Project {project.project_id} Ready for Review",                    message=message,                    channels=["slack"]                )                # Setup await for user response        self._awaiting_review[project.project_id] = asyncio.Event()        async def handle_user_response(self, project_id: str, response: str) -> str:        """        Process user feedback on proposals.        Returns status message.        """        project = await self.repo.load(project_id)        if not project:            return "Project not found."                if project.status != ProjectStatus.PROPOSED:            return f"Project is currently {project.status.name}, cannot modify proposals."                response_lower = response.lower().strip()                # Handle special commands        if response_lower == "cancel":            project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.CANCELLED, "User cancelled")            await self.repo.save(project)            return "Project cancelled."                if response_lower == "execute" or response_lower == "approve all":            # Approve all pending            for p in project.proposals:                if p.approved is None:                    p.approved = True            return await self._finalize_proposals(project)                if response_lower == "reject all":            for p in project.proposals:                p.approved = False            return await self._finalize_proposals(project)                # Parse specific approvals (e.g., "approve 1,3" or "1, 3")        if "approve" in response_lower or "reject" in response_lower:            action = "approve" if "approve" in response_lower else "reject"            # Extract numbers            import re            numbers = re.findall(r'\d+', response)                        for num_str in numbers:                idx = int(num_str) - 1                if 0 <= idx < len(project.proposals):                    project.proposals[idx].approved = (action == "approve")                        await self.repo.save(project)            return f"Updated proposals. {project.get_proposal_summary()}"                # Handle notes        if response_lower.startswith("note:"):            project.user_notes = response[5:].strip()            await self.repo.save(project)            return "Note added. Send 'execute' when ready."                return "I didn't understand. Please use:\n- approve/reject [numbers]\n- approve all/reject all\n- note: [your note]\n- execute\n- cancel"        async def _finalize_proposals(self, project: Project) -> str:        """Finalize proposals and start execution."""        approved = [p for p in project.proposals if p.approved is True]        rejected = [p for p in project.proposals if p.approved is False]                # Calculate final cost        base_cost = 0.10  # Base execution cost estimate        addon_cost = sum(p.additional_cost_usd or 0 for p in approved)        project.estimated_cost_usd = base_cost + addon_cost                project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.APPROVED, f"Approved {len(approved)}/{len(project.proposals)} proposals")        await self.repo.save(project)                # Signal that review is complete        if project.project_id in self._awaiting_review:            self._user_responses[project.project_id] = "execute"            self._awaiting_review[project.project_id].set()                # Start execution        asyncio.create_task(self._execute_project(project.project_id))                summary = f"""✅ *Project Approved: {project.project_id}*Approved enhancements ({len(approved)}):{chr(10).join([f"• {p.title}" for p in approved])}{"Rejected:" + chr(10) + chr(10).join([f"• {p.title}" for p in rejected]) if rejected else ""}Estimated cost: ${project.estimated_cost_usd:.2f}Starting execution...        """                return summary        async def _execute_project(self, project_id: str):        """Execute project with checkpointing."""        project = await self.repo.load(project_id)        if not project or not self.execute_task:            return                project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.RUNNING, "Starting execution")        await self.repo.save(project)                try:            # Create checkpoint before start            project.create_checkpoint({"phase": "start"}, [])                        # Execute with periodic checkpointing            # This would integrate with your existing execution engine            result = await self.execute_task(                project=project,                checkpoint_callback=lambda ctx, res: self._save_checkpoint(project_id, ctx, res)            )                        project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.COMPLETED, "Execution successful")            await self.notifier.success(                title=f"Project {project_id} Complete",                message=str(result)[:500]            )                    except Exception as e:            logger.error("project_execution_failed", project_id=project_id, error=str(e))            project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.FAILED, str(e))                        # Create failure checkpoint for resume            project.create_checkpoint({"error": str(e), "failed_step": project.current_step}, [])                        await self.notifier.error(                title=f"Project {project_id} Failed",                message=str(e),                metadata={"resumable": True, "checkpoints": len(project.checkpoints)}            )                finally:            await self.repo.save(project)        async def _save_checkpoint(self, project_id: str, context: Dict, results: List):        """Save execution checkpoint."""        project = await self.repo.load(project_id)        if project:            project.current_step += 1            cp = project.create_checkpoint(context, results)            project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.CHECKPOINT, f"Step {project.current_step} complete")            await self.repo.save(project)            logger.debug("checkpoint_saved", project_id=project_id, checkpoint_id=cp.checkpoint_id)        async def pause_project(self, project_id: str, reason: str = "User requested"):        """Graceful pause with checkpoint."""        project = await self.repo.load(project_id)        if project and project.status == ProjectStatus.RUNNING:            project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.PAUSED, reason)            await self.repo.save(project)            return True        return False        async def resume_project(self, project_id: str) -> str:        """        Resume project from last checkpoint.        """        project = await self.repo.load(project_id)        if not project:            return "Project not found."                if not project.can_resume():            return f"Cannot resume project in state {project.status.name}"                checkpoint = project.get_latest_checkpoint()                # Restore context        project.transition_to(ProjectStatus.RUNNING, f"Resuming from checkpoint {checkpoint.checkpoint_id}")        await self.repo.save(project)                # Notify        await self.notifier.info(            title=f"Resuming Project {project_id}",            message=f"Restoring from step {checkpoint.step_index}..."        )                # Resume execution        asyncio.create_task(self._execute_project(project_id))                return f"Resuming project from step {checkpoint.step_index}..."        async def list_resumable(self, user_id: str) -> List[Project]:        """Get user's resumable projects."""        return await self.repo.get_resumable(user_id)        async def get_status(self, project_id: str) -> str:        """Get human-readable project status."""        project = await self.repo.load(project_id)        if not project:            return "Project not found."                lines = [            f"📊 *Project {project_id}*",            f"Status: {project.status.name}",            f"Progress: Step {project.current_step}/{len(project.execution_plan) if project.execution_plan else '?'}",            f"Cost: ${project.actual_cost_usd:.2f} / ${project.estimated_cost_usd or '?'}",            f"Checkpoints: {len(project.checkpoints)}",            f"Last updated: {project.updated_at.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}"        ]                if project.can_resume():            lines.append("\n✅ *This project can be resumed*")                return "\n".join(lines)
📄 FILE 21: Bot Integration with Interactive Flow
"""Integration of Project Manager with Telegram and Slack bots.Handles the interactive proposal-review workflow."""from telegram import Update, InlineKeyboardButton, InlineKeyboardMarkupfrom telegram.ext import CallbackQueryHandler, ContextTypesfrom application.services.project_manager import ProjectManagerclass InteractiveBotHandlers:    """    Adds interactive project management to existing bots.    """        def __init__(self, project_manager: ProjectManager):        self.pm = project_manager        def setup_telegram(self, application):        """Add handlers to Telegram bot."""        application.add_handler(CommandHandler("project", self._tg_cmd_project))        application.add_handler(CommandHandler("resume", self._tg_cmd_resume))        application.add_handler(CommandHandler("status", self._tg_cmd_status))        application.add_handler(CallbackQueryHandler(self._tg_callback_handler))        def setup_slack(self, slack_app):        """Add handlers to Slack bot."""        # Add action handlers for proposal buttons        slack_app.action("proposal_approve")(self._slack_proposal_action)        slack_app.action("proposal_reject")(self._slack_proposal_action)        slack_app.action("project_resume")(self._slack_resume_action)        # Telegram Handlers    async def _tg_cmd_project(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE):        """Handle /project command - creates new project with enhancement flow."""        user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)        chat_id = update.effective_chat.id                if not context.args:            await update.message.reply_text(                "Usage: /project <description of what you want to do>\n"                "Example: /project Analyze the sales data and create a PowerPoint presentation"            )            return                request_text = " ".join(context.args)                # Create project        await update.message.reply_text(            f"🎯 Creating project for: _{request_text[:100]}..._\n"            "Analyzing and generating enhancement proposals...",            parse_mode="Markdown"        )                project = await self.pm.create_project(            user_id=user_id,            request=request_text,            channels={"telegram": str(chat_id)}        )                # Setup interactive message for when proposals are ready        # (The ProjectManager will send a notification when analysis completes)        await update.message.reply_text(            f"Project ID: `{project.project_id}`\n"            f"You will receive enhancement proposals shortly.",            parse_mode="Markdown"        )        async def _tg_cmd_resume(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE):        """Handle /resume command."""        user_id = str(update.effective_user.id)                if context.args:            # Resume specific project            project_id = context.args[0]            result = await self.pm.resume_project(project_id)            await update.message.reply_text(result, parse_mode="Markdown")        else:            # List resumable projects            projects = await self.pm.list_resumable(user_id)            if not projects:                await update.message.reply_text("No resumable projects found.")                return                        keyboard = []            for proj in projects:                status_emoji = "⏸️" if proj.status.name == "PAUSED" else "❌"                keyboard.append([                    InlineKeyboardButton(                        f"{status_emoji} {proj.project_id[:8]}... - {proj.user_request[:30]}...",                        callback_data=f"resume:{proj.project_id}"                    )                ])                        await update.message.reply_text(                "Select project to resume:",                reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(keyboard)            )        async def _tg_cmd_status(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE):        """Check project status."""        if not context.args:            await update.message.reply_text("Usage: /status <project_id>")            return                project_id = context.args[0]        status = await self.pm.get_status(project_id)        await update.message.reply_text(status, parse_mode="Markdown")        async def _tg_callback_handler(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE):        """Handle inline button callbacks."""        query = update.callback_query        await query.answer()                data = query.data                if data.startswith("resume:"):            project_id = data.split(":")[1]            result = await self.pm.resume_project(project_id)            await query.edit_message_text(result, parse_mode="Markdown")                elif data.startswith("proposal:"):            # Handle proposal approval/rejection inline            parts = data.split(":")            action, project_id, proposal_idx = parts[0], parts[1], int(parts[2])                        response = f"approve {proposal_idx + 1}" if action == "approve_prop" else f"reject {proposal_idx + 1}"            result = await self.pm.handle_user_response(project_id, response)            await query.edit_message_text(result, parse_mode="Markdown")        # Slack Handlers    async def _slack_proposal_action(self, ack, body, say):        """Handle proposal approve/reject buttons."""        await ack()                action = body["actions"][0]        value = action["value"]  # format: "approve|project_id|idx" or "reject|..."        decision, project_id, idx = value.split("|")                response = f"approve {int(idx) + 1}" if decision == "approve" else f"reject {int(idx) + 1}"        result = await self.pm.handle_user_response(project_id, response)                await say(result)        async def _slack_resume_action(self, ack, body, say):        """Handle resume button."""        await ack()        project_id = body["actions"][0]["value"]        result = await self.pm.resume_project(project_id)        await say(result)# Message router - routes user replies to appropriate projectclass ProjectMessageRouter:    """    Routes incoming messages to projects awaiting user input.    """        def __init__(self, project_manager: ProjectManager):        self.pm = project_manager        # Track which user is reviewing which project        self._user_review_state: Dict[str, str] = {}  # user_id -> project_id        async def handle_message(self, user_id: str, message: str, platform: str) -> Optional[str]:        """        Route message to project if user is in review state.        Returns response or None if not handled.        """        # Check if user has active project awaiting response        if user_id in self._user_review_state:            project_id = self._user_review_state[user_id]            result = await self.pm.handle_user_response(project_id, message)                        # If finalized (execute/cancel), clear state            if "Starting execution" in result or "cancelled" in result.lower():                del self._user_review_state[user_id]                        return result                # Check if this is a new project command        if message.lower().startswith("/project"):            return None  # Let command handler take it                # Check for resume commands        if message.lower().startswith("/resume"):            return None                # If user has projects in PROPOSED status, assume reply is for latest        projects = await self.pm.repo.load_by_user(user_id, ProjectStatus.PROPOSED)        if projects:            latest = projects[0]  # Most recent            self._user_review_state[user_id] = latest.project_id            return await self.pm.handle_user_response(latest.project_id, message)                return None

🔧 Key Features Implemented
Resumable State Machine: Projects persist through crashes, pauses, or failures
Automatic Checkpointing: Every step saved to SQLite with workspace hash
Enhancement Proposals: AI suggests improvements before execution
Interactive Review Loop: User can toggle proposals, add notes, approve/reject
Multi-Platform: Works seamlessly across Telegram and Slack
Cost Transparency: Shows estimated cost before execution based on proposed enhancements
Graceful Recovery: Failed projects can resume from last successful checkpoint

"""Event-Driven Architecture Core.Decouples services via async message passing.Supports: Kafka, RabbitMQ, Redis Pub/Sub (fallback)"""from __future__ import annotationsimport asyncioimport jsonfrom abc import ABC, abstractmethodfrom typing import Callable, Dict, List, Optional, Any, TypeVar, Genericfrom dataclasses import dataclass, asdictfrom datetime import datetimeimport structlogfrom enum import Enum, autoimport aiokafkaimport aio_pikaimport redis.asyncio as redislogger = structlog.get_logger()class EventType(Enum):    """Domain events."""    PROJECT_CREATED = auto()    PROPOSAL_GENERATED = auto()    USER_RESPONDED = auto()    EXECUTION_STARTED = auto()    CHECKPOINT_REACHED = auto()    EXECUTION_COMPLETED = auto()    EXECUTION_FAILED = auto()    LLM_REQUESTED = auto()    LLM_RESPONDED = auto()    TOOL_EXECUTED = auto()    SYSTEM_SCALE_UP = auto()    SYSTEM_SCALE_DOWN = auto()@dataclass(frozen=True)class DomainEvent:    """Immutable domain event."""    event_id: str    event_type: EventType    aggregate_id: str  # Project ID or Entity ID    payload: Dict[str, Any]    timestamp: datetime    service_origin: str    correlation_id: Optional[str] = None  # For distributed tracing    version: int = 1T = TypeVar('T')class MessageBus(ABC):    """Abstract message bus."""        @abstractmethod    async def publish(self, event: DomainEvent) -> None:        pass        @abstractmethod    async def subscribe(        self,         event_types: List[EventType],         handler: Callable[[DomainEvent], None],        consumer_group: Optional[str] = None    ) -> None:        pass        @abstractmethod    async def start(self) -> None:        pass        @abstractmethod    async def stop(self) -> None:        passclass KafkaMessageBus(MessageBus):    """Production-grade Kafka implementation."""        def __init__(self, bootstrap_servers: str = "localhost:9092"):        self.bootstrap_servers = bootstrap_servers        self.producer: Optional[aiokafka.AIOKafkaProducer] = None        self.consumers: List[aiokafka.AIOKafkaConsumer] = []        self._handlers: Dict[EventType, List[Callable]] = {}            async def start(self):        self.producer = aiokafka.AIOKafkaProducer(            bootstrap_servers=self.bootstrap_servers,            value_serializer=lambda v: json.dumps(v, default=str).encode('utf-8'),            key_serializer=lambda k: k.encode('utf-8') if k else None        )        await self.producer.start()        logger.info("kafka_producer_started")        async def stop(self):        if self.producer:            await self.producer.stop()        for consumer in self.consumers:            await consumer.stop()        async def publish(self, event: DomainEvent):        if not self.producer:            raise RuntimeError("Bus not started")                topic = f"manus.{event.event_type.name.lower()}"                await self.producer.send(            topic=topic,            key=event.aggregate_id,            value=asdict(event)        )                logger.debug("event_published", topic=topic, event_id=event.event_id)        async def subscribe(        self,         event_types: List[EventType],         handler: Callable[[DomainEvent], None],        consumer_group: Optional[str] = None    ):        topics = [f"manus.{et.name.lower()}" for et in event_types]                consumer = aiokafka.AIOKafkaConsumer(            *topics,            bootstrap_servers=self.bootstrap_servers,            group_id=consumer_group or "manus-default",            value_deserializer=lambda v: json.loads(v.decode('utf-8')),            auto_offset_reset='earliest'        )                await consumer.start()        self.consumers.append(consumer)                # Start consumption loop        asyncio.create_task(self._consume_loop(consumer, handler))        async def _consume_loop(self, consumer: aiokafka.AIOKafkaConsumer, handler: Callable):        async for msg in consumer:            try:                event = DomainEvent(**msg.value)                await handler(event)            except Exception as e:                logger.error("event_handler_failed", error=str(e), msg=msg.value)class InMemoryMessageBus(MessageBus):    """For testing and single-node deployments."""        def __init__(self):        self._subscribers: Dict[EventType, List[Callable]] = {}        self._queue: asyncio.Queue = asyncio.Queue()        self._running = False            async def start(self):        self._running = True        asyncio.create_task(self._dispatch_loop())        async def stop(self):        self._running = False        async def publish(self, event: DomainEvent):        await self._queue.put(event)        async def subscribe(        self,         event_types: List[EventType],         handler: Callable[[DomainEvent], None],        consumer_group: Optional[str] = None    ):        for et in event_types:            if et not in self._subscribers:                self._subscribers[et] = []            self._subscribers[et].append(handler)        async def _dispatch_loop(self):        while self._running:            event = await self._queue.get()            handlers = self._subscribers.get(event.event_type, [])            for handler in handlers:                try:                    asyncio.create_task(handler(event))                except Exception as e:                    logger.error("handler_error", error=str(e))class EventSourcingRepository(Generic[T]):    """    Event sourcing for aggregates.    Reconstruct state from event stream.    """        def __init__(self, bus: MessageBus, snapshot_store: Optional[Any] = None):        self.bus = bus        self.snapshot_store = snapshot_store        self._aggregates: Dict[str, T] = {}  # In-memory cache        async def save(self, aggregate_id: str, events: List[DomainEvent]):        for event in events:            await self.bus.publish(event)                # Snapshot every 10 events        if len(events) % 10 == 0 and self.snapshot_store:            await self._create_snapshot(aggregate_id)        async def load(self, aggregate_id: str) -> Optional[T]:        # Try cache        if aggregate_id in self._aggregates:            return self._aggregates[aggregate_id]                # Reconstruct from events (simplified)        # In production: Read from event store (CockroachDB/EventStoreDB)        return None        async def _create_snapshot(self, aggregate_id: str):        pass
📄 FILE 24: infrastructure/plugins/registry.py
"""Plugin Architecture for Dynamic Tool Loading.Supports hot-reloading, versioned tools, and isolated execution contexts."""from __future__ import annotationsimport importlibimport importlib.utilimport inspectimport pkgutilimport sysfrom abc import ABC, abstractmethodfrom typing import Dict, List, Type, Optional, Any, Callablefrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom pathlib import Pathimport asyncioimport structlogimport hashlibfrom contextlib import contextmanagerlogger = structlog.get_logger()class ToolInterface(ABC):    """Contract for all tools."""        @property    @abstractmethod    def name(self) -> str:        pass        @property    @abstractmethod    def version(self) -> str:        pass        @property    @abstractmethod    def capabilities(self) -> List[str]:        pass        @abstractmethod    async def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any], context: ToolContext) -> ToolResult:        pass        @abstractmethod    def health_check(self) -> bool:        pass@dataclassclass ToolContext:    """Execution context passed to tools."""    project_id: str    workspace_path: Path    cancellation_token: asyncio.Event    memory_limit_mb: int    timeout_seconds: int    audit_logger: Any@dataclassclass ToolResult:    success: bool    data: Any    logs: List[str]    metrics: Dict[str, float]  # execution_time_ms, memory_peak_mb, etc.    artifacts: List[Path] = None@dataclassclass PluginMetadata:    name: str    version: str    author: str    dependencies: List[str]    entry_point: str    hash: str  # For integrity verification    sandbox_required: bool = Trueclass PluginRegistry:    """    Dynamic plugin loader with isolation.    Supports loading from:    - Local Python packages    - Wheel files (.whl)    - Git repositories    - Docker images (for external tools)    """        def __init__(self, plugin_dirs: List[Path], sandbox_enabled: bool = True):        self.plugin_dirs = plugin_dirs        self.sandbox_enabled = sandbox_enabled        self._tools: Dict[str, ToolInterface] = {}        self._metadata: Dict[str, PluginMetadata] = {}        self._hooks: Dict[str, List[Callable]] = {            'pre_execute': [],            'post_execute': [],            'on_load': [],            'on_unload': []        }            async def discover(self):        """Auto-discover plugins in directories."""        for directory in self.plugin_dirs:            if not directory.exists():                continue                        for item in directory.iterdir():                if item.is_dir() and (item / "__init__.py").exists():                    await self._load_from_directory(item)                elif item.suffix == ".py" and item.name != "__init__.py":                    await self._load_from_file(item)                elif item.suffix == ".whl":                    await self._load_from_wheel(item)        async def _load_from_directory(self, path: Path):        """Load Python package as plugin."""        module_name = f"manus_plugins.{path.name}"                try:            spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(                module_name,                 path / "__init__.py"            )            module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)            sys.modules[module_name] = module            spec.loader.exec_module(module)                        # Find ToolInterface implementations            for name, obj in inspect.getmembers(module):                if (inspect.isclass(obj) and                     issubclass(obj, ToolInterface) and                     obj != ToolInterface):                                        instance = obj()                    await self.register(instance)                            except Exception as e:            logger.error("plugin_load_failed", path=str(path), error=str(e))        async def _load_from_file(self, path: Path):        """Load single Python file as plugin."""        spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(            f"manus_plugins.{path.stem}",             path        )        module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)        spec.loader.exec_module(module)        # ... similar to directory loading        async def _load_from_wheel(self, path: Path):        """Install and load wheel."""        import subprocess        subprocess.check_call([sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", str(path)])        # Then discover entry points        async def register(self, tool: ToolInterface, metadata: Optional[PluginMetadata] = None):        """Register a tool instance."""        if tool.name in self._tools:            logger.warning("tool_override", name=tool.name)                self._tools[tool.name] = tool                if not metadata:            metadata = PluginMetadata(                name=tool.name,                version=tool.version,                author="unknown",                dependencies=[],                entry_point=f"{tool.__class__.__module__}.{tool.__class__.__name__}",                hash=self._calculate_hash(tool)            )                self._metadata[tool.name] = metadata                # Trigger hooks        for hook in self._hooks['on_load']:            await hook(tool)                logger.info("tool_registered", name=tool.name, version=tool.version)        def unregister(self, name: str):        """Hot-unload a tool."""        if name in self._tools:            tool = self._tools.pop(name)            for hook in self._hooks['on_unload']:                asyncio.create_task(hook(tool))            logger.info("tool_unregistered", name=name)        async def execute(        self,         tool_name: str,         params: Dict[str, Any],         context: ToolContext    ) -> ToolResult:        """        Execute tool with pre/post hooks and sandboxing.        """        tool = self._tools.get(tool_name)        if not tool:            raise ToolNotFoundError(f"Tool {tool_name} not found")                # Pre-execution hooks        for hook in self._hooks['pre_execute']:            await hook(tool, params, context)                # Execute with sandbox if required        metadata = self._metadata[tool_name]        if metadata.sandbox_required and self.sandbox_enabled:            result = await self._execute_sandboxed(tool, params, context)        else:            result = await tool.execute(params, context)                # Post-execution hooks        for hook in self._hooks['post_execute']:            await hook(tool, result)                return result        async def _execute_sandboxed(        self,         tool: ToolInterface,         params: Dict,         context: ToolContext    ) -> ToolResult:        """Execute in restricted subprocess."""        # Implementation using ProcessPoolExecutor        # with resource limits (memory, CPU, network)        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()        return await loop.run_in_executor(            None,  # Use default executor            self._subprocess_execute,            tool,            params,            context        )        def _subprocess_execute(self, tool, params, context):        """Actual subprocess execution (CPU-bound isolation)."""        # Spawn new Python process with limited resources        # using multiprocessing        pass        def _calculate_hash(self, tool: ToolInterface) -> str:        """Calculate integrity hash."""        source = inspect.getsource(tool.__class__)        return hashlib.sha256(source.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]        def register_hook(self, event: str, callback: Callable):        """Register lifecycle hook."""        if event in self._hooks:            self._hooks[event].append(callback)        def list_tools(self) -> List[Dict]:        """List available tools."""        return [            {                "name": name,                "version": tool.version,                "capabilities": tool.capabilities,                "healthy": tool.health_check()            }            for name, tool in self._tools.items()        ]        def get_tool(self, name: str) -> Optional[ToolInterface]:        return self._tools.get(name)class ToolNotFoundError(Exception):    pass
📄 FILE 25: services/orchestrator_service.py
"""Stateless Orchestration Service.Can be horizontally scaled behind load balancer.Uses event sourcing for state persistence."""from __future__ import annotationsimport asynciofrom typing import Dict, Optional, Listfrom dataclasses import dataclassimport structlogfrom infrastructure.messaging.event_bus import MessageBus, DomainEvent, EventTypefrom infrastructure.plugins.registry import PluginRegistrylogger = structlog.get_logger()@dataclassclass ScaleMetrics:    """Auto-scaling triggers."""    queue_depth: int    cpu_percent: float    memory_percent: float    active_projects: intclass OrchestratorService:    """    Stateless project orchestrator.    - Receives commands via Message Bus    - Maintains no in-memory state (uses event store)    - Horizontally scalable    """        def __init__(        self,        event_bus: MessageBus,        plugin_registry: PluginRegistry,        instance_id: Optional[str] = None    ):        self.bus = event_bus        self.plugins = plugin_registry        self.instance_id = instance_id or f"orch-{asyncio.get_event_loop().time()}"        self._shutting_down = False                # Local cache of active projects (volatile, reconstructable from events)        self._active_projects: Dict[str, dict] = {}        async def start(self):        """Subscribe to events."""        await self.bus.subscribe(            [EventType.PROJECT_CREATED, EventType.USER_RESPONDED, EventType.EXECUTION_FAILED],            self._handle_project_event,            consumer_group="orchestrators"  # Load balancing across instances        )                # Start health reporter        asyncio.create_task(self._health_reporter())                logger.info("orchestrator_started", instance_id=self.instance_id)        async def _handle_project_event(self, event: DomainEvent):        """Event handler (idempotent)."""        if self._shutting_down:            return                project_id = event.aggregate_id                # Check if we should handle this (consistent hashing for locality)        if not self._should_handle(project_id):            return                try:            if event.event_type == EventType.PROJECT_CREATED:                await self._on_project_created(event)            elif event.event_type == EventType.USER_RESPONDED:                await self._on_user_response(event)            elif event.event_type == EventType.EXECUTION_FAILED:                await self._on_execution_failed(event)                        except Exception as e:            logger.error("event_handler_failed", error=str(e), event_type=event.event_type)            # Publish to dead letter queue        def _should_handle(self, project_id: str) -> bool:        """        Consistent hashing to distribute projects across instances.        Ensures same project always handled by same instance (locality).        """        import hashlib        hash_val = int(hashlib.md5(project_id.encode()).hexdigest(), 16)        # In real deployment: check against instance ring        return True  # Simplified        async def _on_project_created(self, event: DomainEvent):        """Start enhancement analysis."""        project_id = event.aggregate_id                # Publish command to cognitive service        await self.bus.publish(DomainEvent(            event_id=f"{self.instance_id}_{asyncio.get_event_loop().time()}",            event_type=EventType.PROPOSAL_GENERATED,            aggregate_id=project_id,            payload={"command": "analyze_and_propose", "params": event.payload},            timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),            service_origin=self.instance_id        ))        async def _on_user_response(self, event: DomainEvent):        """Handle user approval/rejection."""        response = event.payload.get("response")                if "execute" in response.lower():            # Start execution across multiple workers            await self._distribute_execution(event.aggregate_id)        async def _distribute_execution(self, project_id: str):        """Shard execution steps across worker pool."""        # Load execution plan        steps = await self._load_execution_plan(project_id)                # Publish step commands to worker queue        for idx, step in enumerate(steps):            await self.bus.publish(DomainEvent(                event_id=f"{project_id}_step_{idx}",                event_type=EventType.EXECUTION_STARTED,                aggregate_id=project_id,                payload={"step_index": idx, "step_data": step},                timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),                service_origin=self.instance_id            ))        async def _health_reporter(self):        """Report metrics for auto-scaling."""        while not self._shutting_down:            metrics = ScaleMetrics(                queue_depth=len(self._active_projects),                cpu_percent=psutil.cpu_percent(),                memory_percent=psutil.virtual_memory().percent,                active_projects=len(self._active_projects)            )                        # Publish metrics to monitoring            await self.bus.publish(DomainEvent(                event_id=f"metrics_{self.instance_id}",                event_type=EventType.SYSTEM_SCALE_UP if metrics.queue_depth > 100 else EventType.SYSTEM_SCALE_DOWN,                aggregate_id=self.instance_id,                payload=asdict(metrics),                timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),                service_origin=self.instance_id            ))                        await asyncio.sleep(30)  # Report every 30s        async def shutdown(self):        """Graceful shutdown."""        self._shutting_down = True        # Wait for active projects to reach checkpoint        await asyncio.sleep(5)

📄 FILE 28: configuration/service_mesh.py
"""Service Mesh Configuration for inter-service communication.Handles: Load balancing, retries, timeouts, circuit breaking."""from dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, Optionalimport asyncioimport random@dataclassclass ServiceEndpoint:    host: str    port: int    weight: int = 100    healthy: bool = True    current_connections: int = 0class LoadBalancer:    """Pluggable load balancing strategies."""        def __init__(self, strategy: str = "round_robin"):        self.strategy = strategy        self.endpoints: List[ServiceEndpoint] = []        self._rr_index = 0        def add_endpoint(self, endpoint: ServiceEndpoint):        self.endpoints.append(endpoint)        def get_endpoint(self) -> Optional[ServiceEndpoint]:        healthy = [e for e in self.endpoints if e.healthy]        if not healthy:            return None                if self.strategy == "round_robin":            endpoint = healthy[self._rr_index % len(healthy)]            self._rr_index += 1            return endpoint                elif self.strategy == "least_connections":            return min(healthy, key=lambda e: e.current_connections)                elif self.strategy == "weighted_random":            total = sum(e.weight for e in healthy)            r = random.uniform(0, total)            upto = 0            for e in healthy:                upto += e.weight                if upto >= r:                    return e                return healthy[0]class CircuitBreaker:    """Distributed circuit breaker."""        def __init__(self, redis_client, failure_threshold: int = 5, timeout: int = 60):        self.redis = redis_client        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold        self.timeout = timeout        async def call(self, service_name: str, coro):        """Execute with circuit breaker protection."""        key = f"circuit:{service_name}"                # Check state        state = await self.redis.get(key)        if state == b"OPEN":            raise CircuitBreakerOpen(f"Circuit open for {service_name}")                try:            result = await coro            # Success - reset counter            await self.redis.delete(f"{key}:failures")            return result                    except Exception as e:            # Increment failure count            failures = await self.redis.incr(f"{key}:failures")            if failures >= self.failure_threshold:                await self.redis.setex(key, self.timeout, "OPEN")            raise

"""Unified Browser Automation Interface.Supports Playwright (primary) and Puppeteer (fallback/legacy).Intelligent selection based on task requirements."""from __future__ import annotationsimport asyncioimport subprocessfrom abc import ABC, abstractmethodfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List, Callable, AsyncIterator, Literalfrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom enum import Enum, autofrom pathlib import Pathimport structlogimport tempfileimport timefrom contextlib import asynccontextmanagerimport base64logger = structlog.get_logger()class BrowserType(Enum):    CHROMIUM = "chromium"    FIREFOX = "firefox"    WEBKIT = "webkit"    CHROME = "chrome"class AutomationEngine(Enum):    """Available automation backends."""        await asyncio.sleep(0.5)                        return {                "status": response.status if response else 0,                "url": response.url if response else options.url bool:        return self._page is not None and not self._page.is_closed()class PuppeteerAdapter(BaseBrowserAdapter):    """    Puppeteer implementation.
