initialize(self):        """Connect to Redis or setup local storage."""        if self.redis_url:            try:                self._redis = redis.from_url(self.redis_url, decode_responses=True)                await self._redis.ping()                logger.info("heartbeat_redis_connected")            except:                logger.warning("redis_unavailable_using_memory")                self._redis = None        async def register_process(        self,        process_id: str,        process_type: str,        metadata: Optional[Dict] = None,        on_failure: Optional[Callable] = None    ) -> "ProcessHeartbeat":        """Register a process for monitoring."""        entry = HeartbeatEntry(            process_id=process_id,            process_type=process_type,            status=ProcessStatus.HEALTHY,            last_beat=time.time(),            metadata=metadata or {}        )                await self._store_entry(entry)                if on_failure:            self._callbacks[process_id] = on_failure                logger.info("process_registered", process_id=process_id, type=process_type)                return ProcessHeartbeat(self, process_id)        async def _store_entry(self, entry: HeartbeatEntry):        """Store entry in Redis or memory."""        data = {            "process_id": entry.process_id,            "process_type": entry.process_type,            "status": entry.status.name,            "last_beat": entry.last_beat,            "consecutive_misses": entry.consecutive_misses,            "metadata": orjson.dumps(entry.metadata).decode()        }                if self._redis:            key = f"heartbeat:{entry.process_id}"            await self._redis.hset(key, mapping=data)            await self._redis.expire(key, int(self.heartbeat_interval * 4))        else:            self._local_store[entry.process_id] = entry        async def _get_entry(self, process_id: str) -> Optional[HeartbeatEntry]:        """Retrieve entry."""        if self._redis:            key = f"heartbeat:{process_id}"            data = await self._redis.hgetall(key)            if not data:                return None            return HeartbeatEntry(                process_id=data["process_id"],                process_type=data["process_type"],                status=ProcessStatus[data["status"]],                last_beat=float(data["last_beat"]),                consecutive_misses=int(data["consecutive_misses"]),                metadata=orjson.loads(data["metadata"])            )        else:            return self._local_store.get(process_id)        async def start_monitoring(self):        """Start monitoring loop."""        self._running = True                while self._running:            try:                await self._check_all_processes()                await asyncio.sleep(self.check_interval)            except Exception as e:                logger.error("heartbeat_check_error", error=str(e))        async def _check_all_processes(self):        """Check all registered processes."""        now = time.time()        threshold = self.heartbeat_interval * 2  # 2 missed beats = warning                # Get all processes        if self._redis:            keys = await self._redis.keys("heartbeat:*")            entries = []            for key in keys:                data = await self._redis.hgetall(key)                if data:                    entries.append(HeartbeatEntry(                        process_id=data["process_id"],                        process_type=data["process_type"],                        status=ProcessStatus[data["status"]],                        last_beat=float(data["last_beat"]),                        consecutive_misses=int(data.get("consecutive_misses", 0)),                        metadata=orjson.loads(data.get("metadata", "{}"))                    ))        else:            entries = list(self._local_store.values())                for entry in entries:            time_since_beat = now - entry.last_beat                        if time_since_beat > threshold:                entry.consecutive_misses += 1                                if entry.consecutive_misses >= entry.max_misses:                    entry.status = ProcessStatus.FAILED                    logger.error(                        "process_declared_dead",                        process_id=entry.process_id,                        last_beat=entry.last_beat,                        misses=entry.consecutive_misses                    )                                        # Trigger callback                    if entry.process_id in self._callbacks:                        try:                            await self._callbacks[entry.process_id](entry)                        except Exception as e:                            logger.error("failure_callback_error", error=str(e))                                        # Cleanup                    await self._remove_entry(entry.process_id)                                    else:                    entry.status = ProcessStatus.WARNING if entry.consecutive_misses == 1 else ProcessStatus.CRITICAL                    logger.warning(                        "process_missed_heartbeat",                        process_id=entry.process_id,                        misses=entry.consecutive_misses                    )                    await self._store_entry(entry)        async def _remove_entry(self, process_id: str):        """Remove process from monitoring."""        if self._redis:            await self._redis.delete(f"heartbeat:{process_id}")        else:            self._local_store.pop(process_id, None)        self._callbacks.pop(process_id, None)        def stop(self):        """Stop monitoring."""        self._running = False        async def get_cluster_health(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Get overall cluster health."""        if self._redis:            keys = await self._redis.keys("heartbeat:*")            total = len(keys)            healthy = 0            warning = 0            critical = 0                        for key in keys:                data = await self._redis.hgetall(key)                status = data.get("status", "UNKNOWN")                if status == "HEALTHY":                    healthy += 1                elif status == "WARNING":                    warning += 1                elif status in ["CRITICAL", "FAILED"]:                    critical += 1                        return {                "total_processes": total,                "healthy": healthy,                "warning": warning,                "critical": critical,                "health_percentage": (healthy / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0            }        else:            return {                "total_processes": len(self._local_store),                "healthy": sum(1 for e in self._local_store.values() if e.status == ProcessStatus.HEALTHY)            }class ProcessHeartbeat:    """    Context manager για individual process heartbeat.    """        def __init__(self, manager: HeartbeatManager, process_id: str):        self.manager = manager        self.process_id = process_id        self._task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None        self._running = False            async def __aenter__(self):        """Start heartbeat."""        self._running = True        self._task = asyncio.create_task(self._beat_loop())        return self        async def __aexit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):        """Stop heartbeat."""        self._running = False        if self._task:            self._task.cancel()            try:                await self._task            except asyncio.CancelledError:                pass        async def _beat_loop(self):        """Send periodic heartbeats."""        while self._running:            try:                await self._send_beat()                await asyncio.sleep(self.manager.heartbeat_interval)            except asyncio.CancelledError:                break            except Exception as e:                logger.error("heartbeat_send_error", error=str(e))                await asyncio.sleep(1)        async def _send_beat(self):        """Update heartbeat timestamp."""        entry = await self.manager._get_entry(self.process_id)        if entry:            entry.last_beat = time.time()            entry.consecutive_misses = 0            entry.status = ProcessStatus.HEALTHY            await self.manager._store_entry(entry)        async def update_metadata(self, metadata: Dict[str, Any]):        """Update process metadata."""        entry = await self.manager._get_entry(self.process_id)        if entry:            entry.metadata.update(metadata)            await self.manager._store_entry(entry)        async def checkpoint(self, data: Dict[str, Any]):        """Save checkpoint data for resume."""        # Store in Redis for persistence        if self.manager._redis:            key = f"checkpoint:{self.process_id}"            await self.manager._redis.setex(                key,                86400,  # 24 hour retention                orjson.dumps(data)            )            logger.debug("checkpoint_saved", process_id=self.process_id)
📄 FILE 42: infrastructure/vector_db/chroma_integration.py
"""Vector Database Integration for semantic storage of scraped content.Uses ChromaDB (embedded, zero-config) or Qdrant (distributed)."""from __future__ import annotationsfrom typing import List, Dict, Optional, Any, Callablefrom dataclasses import dataclassimport hashlibimport structlogimport numpy as npfrom datetime import datetimelogger = structlog.get_logger()@dataclassclass Document:    """Document for vector storage."""    id: str    content: str    metadata: Dict[str, Any]    embedding: Optional[List[float]] = Noneclass VectorStore:    """    Unified vector database interface.    Supports ChromaDB (local) and Qdrant (distributed).    """        def __init__(        self,        collection_name: str = "manus_content",        embedding_function: Optional[Callable] = None,        persist_directory: Optional[str] = "./data/vector_db"    ):        self.collection_name = collection_name        self.persist_directory = persist_directory        self._embedding_fn = embedding_function or self._default_embedding                self._client = None        self._collection = None            async def initialize(self):        """Initialize ChromaDB."""        try:            import chromadb            from chromadb.config import Settings                        self._client = chromadb.PersistentClient(                path=self.persist_directory,                settings=Settings(                    anonymized_telemetry=False,                    allow_reset=True                )            )                        # Get or create collection            self._collection = self._client.get_or_create_collection(                name=self.collection_name,                metadata={"hnsw:space": "cosine"}            )                        logger.info("vector_db_initialized", collection=self.collection_name)                    except ImportError:            logger.error("chromadb_not_installed")            raise        async def add_documents(        self,        documents: List[Document],        batch_size: int = 100    ):        """        Add documents with embeddings.        """        if not self._collection:            await self.initialize()                # Generate embeddings if not provided        for doc in documents:            if doc.embedding is None:                doc.embedding = await self._embedding_fn(doc.content)                # Batch add        for i in range(0, len(documents), batch_size):            batch = documents[i:i + batch_size]                        ids = [doc.id for doc in batch]            texts = [doc.content for doc in batch]            embeddings = [doc.embedding for doc in batch]            metadatas = [doc.metadata for doc in batch]                        self._collection.add(                ids=ids,                documents=texts,                embeddings=embeddings,                metadatas=metadatas            )                        logger.debug("documents_added", count=len(batch))        async def search(        self,        query: str,        n_results: int = 5,        filter_dict: Optional[Dict] = None,        min_similarity: float = 0.7    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:        """        Semantic search with metadata filtering.        """        if not self._collection:            await self.initialize()                # Embed query        query_embedding = await self._embedding_fn(query)                # Search        results = self._collection.query(            query_embeddings=[query_embedding],            n_results=n_results,            where=filter_dict,            include=["documents", "metadatas", "distances"]        )                # Format results        formatted = []        for i in range(len(results["ids"][0])):            similarity = 1 - results["distances"][0][i]  # Convert distance to similarity                        if similarity >= min_similarity:                formatted.append({                    "id": results["ids"][0][i],                    "content": results["documents"][0][i],                    "metadata": results["metadatas"][0][i],                    "similarity": round(similarity, 4)                })                # Sort by similarity        formatted.sort(key=lambda x: x["similarity"], reverse=True)        return formatted        async def hybrid_search(        self,        query: str,        keywords: List[str],        n_results: int = 5    ) -> List[Dict]:        """        Combined vector + keyword search.        """        # Vector search        vector_results = await self.search(query, n_results=n_results * 2)                # Keyword boost        keyword_set = set(k.lower() for k in keywords)                for result in vector_results:            content_lower = result["content"].lower()            keyword_matches = sum(1 for k in keyword_set if k in content_lower)            # Boost score based on keyword matches            result["similarity"] += (keyword_matches * 0.05)                # Re-sort and return top        vector_results.sort(key=lambda x: x["similarity"], reverse=True)        return vector_results[:n_results]        async def update_document(self, doc_id: str, new_content: str, new_metadata: Optional[Dict] = None):        """Update existing document."""        if not self._collection:            return                # Delete old        self._collection.delete(ids=[doc_id])                # Add new        new_doc = Document(            id=doc_id,            content=new_content,            metadata=new_metadata or {},            embedding=await self._embedding_fn(new_content)        )                await self.add_documents([new_doc])        async def delete_by_filter(self, filter_dict: Dict[str, Any]):        """Delete documents matching filter."""        if self._collection:            self._collection.delete(where=filter_dict)        async def get_stats(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Collection statistics."""        if not self._collection:            return {}                return {            "document_count": self._collection.count(),            "collection_name": self.collection_name,            "embedding_dimension": 384  # Depends on model used        }        async def _default_embedding(self, text: str) -> List[float]:        """        Default embedding using sentence-transformers (local).        Falls back to hash-based pseudo-embedding if model not available.        """        try:            from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer                        if not hasattr(self, '_model'):                # Lightweight model, ~100MB                self._model = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')                        embedding = self._model.encode(text, convert_to_tensor=False)            return embedding.tolist()                    except ImportError:            # Fallback: simple hash-based (not semantic, but deterministic)            logger.warning("sentence_transformers_not_available")            return self._hash_embedding(text)        def _hash_embedding(self, text: str, dim: int = 384) -> List[float]:        """Deterministic hash-based embedding (fallback)."""        import hashlib        np.random.seed(int(hashlib.md5(text.encode()).hexdigest(), 16) % (2**32))        vec = np.random.randn(dim)        return (vec / np.linalg.norm(vec)).tolist()# Integration with scrapingclass ScrapingVectorPipeline:    """    Automatic vectorization of scraped content.    """        def __init__(self, vector_store: VectorStore):        self.store = vector_store            async def process_scrape_result(self, result: Dict[str, Any], source_url: str):        """Store scraped content in vector DB."""        if not result.get("text"):            return                # Chunk large texts        chunks = self._chunk_text(result["text"], chunk_size=500, overlap=50)                documents = []        for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):            doc_id = hashlib.blake2b(                f"{source_url}_{i}".encode()            ).hexdigest()                        documents.append(Document(                id=doc_id,                content=chunk,                metadata={                    "source_url": source_url,                    "title": result.get("title", ""),                    "chunk_index": i,                    "total_chunks": len(chunks),                    "scraped_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),                    "status_code": result.get("status", 0)                }            ))                await self.store.add_documents(documents)        logger.info("content_vectorized", url=source_url, chunks=len(chunks))        def _chunk_text(self, text: str, chunk_size: int = 500, overlap: int = 50) -> List[str]:        """Split text into overlapping chunks."""        words = text.split()        chunks = []                for i in range(0, len(words), chunk_size - overlap):            chunk = " ".join(words[i:i + chunk_size])            if len(chunk) > 50:  # Min chunk size                chunks.append(chunk)                return chunks
📄 FILE 43: Integration with Heartbeat + Vector DB
# Example usage in orchestrator:class ResilientScrapingOrchestrator:    """    Orchestrator with heartbeat monitoring και vector storage.    """        def __init__(self):        self.heartbeat = HeartbeatManager(redis_url="redis://localhost")        self.vector_pipeline = ScrapingVectorPipeline(VectorStore())        self.static_scraper = OptimizedStaticScraper()        self.dynamic_scraper = OptimizedDynamicScraper()            async def execute_long_scraping_task(self, urls: List[str], task_id: str):        """        Execute with full monitoring και semantic storage.        """        # Register with heartbeat        async with await self.heartbeat.register_process(            process_id=f"scrape_{task_id}",            process_type="bulk_scraper",            metadata={"url_count": len(urls), "started_at": time.time()},            on_failure=self._handle_scraper_failure        ) as hb:                        results = []                        for i, url in enumerate(urls):                # Update progress in heartbeat metadata                await hb.update_metadata({                    "progress": f"{i}/{len(urls)}",                    "current_url": url                })                                # Checkpoint every 10 URLs                if i % 10 == 0:                    await hb.checkpoint({                        "completed_urls": urls[:i],                        "results_so_far": results[-10:] if results else []                    })                                # Scrape                result = await self.static_scraper.scrape(url)                results.append(result)                                # Store in vector DB for RAG                await self.vector_pipeline.process_scrape_result(result, url)                                # Small delay to be polite                await asyncio.sleep(0.5)                        return results        async def _handle_scraper_failure(self, entry: HeartbeatEntry):        """Recovery logic when scraper fails."""        logger.error("scraper_died_recovering", process_id=entry.process_id)                # Load checkpoint        checkpoint_key = f"checkpoint:{entry.process_id}"        checkpoint_data = await self.heartbeat._redis.get(checkpoint_key)                if checkpoint_data:            data = orjson.loads(checkpoint_data)            completed = data.get("completed_urls", [])            remaining = [url for url in entry.metadata.get("urls", []) if url not in completed]                        # Restart task with remaining URLs            logger.info("restarting_from_checkpoint", remaining=len(remaining))            asyncio.create_task(                self.execute_long_scraping_task(remaining, entry.process_id.replace("scrape_", ""))            )# Health monitoring endpointasync def get_system_health():    """Aggregate health από όλα subsystems."""    return {        "cluster": await heartbeat.get_cluster_health(),        "vector_db": await vector_store.get_stats(),        "scraping_queues": {            "static_pending": len(static_scraper.cache),            "dynamic_contexts": len(dynamic_scraper._contexts)        },        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()    }

# Αρχιτεκτονική Επικοινωνίας Χρήστη## User Interaction Architecture### 1. Μοντέλο Επικοινωνίας: "Collaborative Agent"Το Manus-Win11 χρησιμοποιεί **υβριδικό μοντέλο** επικοινωνίας:- **Proactive**: Ο agent προτείνει, ρωτάει για clarifications, στέλνει ενημερώσεις- **Reactive**: Απαντάει σε εντολές, εκτελεί αιτήματα- **Asynchronous**: Μακροχρόνιες εργασίες τρέχουν στο background με ενημερώσεις progress
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │ ΧΡΗΣΤΗΣ │ │ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ │ │ │ Telegram │ │ Slack │ │ Email │ │ │ └──────┬───────┘ └──────┬───────┘ └──────┬───────┘ │ └─────────┼─────────────────┼─────────────────┼──────────────┘ │ │ │ └─────────────────┼─────────────────┘ │ ┌───────────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐ │ UNIFIED CONVERSATION LAYER │ │ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ │ │ │ Intent │ │ Context │ │ Session │ │ │ │ Parser │ │ Manager │ │ State │ │ │ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ │ └───────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┘ │ ┌───────────────────────────▼────────────────────────────────┐ │ AGENT COGNITIVE LAYER │ │ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ │ │ │ Planning │ │ Execution │ │ Reflection │ │ │ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ │ └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
### 2. Καταστάσεις Συνομιλίας (Conversation States)Κάθε αλληλεπίδραση περνάει από καθορισμένες καταστάσεις:```pythonclass ConversationState(Enum):    IDLE = auto()              # Αναμονή για είσοδο    CLARIFYING = auto()        # Ζητάει διευκρινίσεις    PROPOSING = auto()         # Παρουσιάζει enhancement proposals    CONFIRMING = auto()        # Περιμένει έγκριση (safety critical)    EXECUTING = auto()         # Εκτελεί task (background)    REPORTING = auto()         # Παρουσιάζει αποτελέσματα    ERROR_RECOVERY = auto()    # Χειρισμός σφάλματος + προτάσεις    PAUSED = auto()            # Διακοπή για human input
3. Τύποι Αλληλεπίδρασης
Α. Command Mode (Εντολές)
Χρήστης: /task Analyze Q3 sales data and create chartsAgent:   🎯 Project #123 created         Analyzing requirements...         [5" αργότερα]         📋 Proposals ready:         1. Include trend analysis? [Yes/No]         2. Export to PDF? [Yes/No]

Χρήστης: Θέλω να φτιάξω ένα script για τα data μουAgent:   Ποια data; (CSV, JSON, database;)Χρήστης: CSV με salesAgent:   Τι ανάλυση χρειάζεσαι; (summary, trends, forecasting;)Χρήστης: TrendsAgent:   [Προτείνει enhancements...]
C. Proactive Mode (Πρωτοβουλία)
Agent:   ⚠️ Project #122 failed at step 3/5         Error: Network timeout         💡 Suggestions:         1. Retry with longer timeout         2. Skip failed item and continue         3. Cancel and review         Χρήστης: 1Agent:   ✅ Resuming from checkpoint...
4. Διαχείριση Context Across Channels
Ο χρήστης μπορεί να αλλάζει κανάλι και η συνομιλία συνεχίζεται:
Session Persistence:  - Session ID: user_123_abc  - Active Projects: [proj_456, proj_789]  - Last Channel: telegram  - Pending Approvals: [approval_001]  Channel Switch Example:  1. User starts task on Telegram  2. Switches to Slack: "/status proj_456"  3. Agent responds on Slack with current status  4. User approves proposal via Slack  5. Agent continues execution (started on Telegram, approved on Slack)
5. Rich Interaction Components
Interactive Elements ανά Κανάλι:
Telegram:
Inline keyboards (Yes/No/Custom)
Callback buttons (Approve/Reject/Modify)
Progress bars (edit message every 10%)
File uploads (drag & drop support)
Slack:
Block Kit UI (structured forms)
Modal dialogs (για complex input)
Thread-based conversations (κάθε project σε thread)
Slash commands με autocomplete
Email (Optional):
Structured HTML reports
Action buttons (deep links to web UI)
Daily digests (batch notifications)
6. Human-in-the-Loop Workflows
Workflow A: Approval Required
Agent:   🔒 Critical Action Required         Action: Delete file "important_data.csv"         Risk: High (irreversible)                  [Approve] [Reject] [View Alternatives]         Χρήστης: [Click Approve]Agent:   ✅ Approved by user at 14:32         Executing...
Workflow B: Clarification Loop
Agent:   ❓ Ambiguity detected         "Process the files" could mean:         1. All files in /workspace         2. Only .csv files         3. Files modified today                  Reply with number or be more specific:         Χρήστης: 2 (only CSV)Agent:   ✅ Processing 12 CSV files...
Workflow C: Enhancement Negotiation
Agent:   💡 I can make this better:         Current request: "Download webpage"         Enhancement: "Extract article text + images + save as PDF"         Additional cost: $0.02         Time: +15 seconds                  Accept? [Yes] [No] [Modify]
7. Notification Strategy (Smart Batching)
NotificationPriority:  CRITICAL: Immediate (DM + Sound + Mobile Push)    - Project failed    - Security alert    - Budget exceeded      HIGH: Within 1 minute    - Step completed (if user waiting)    - Approval required    - Error with retry options      NORMAL: Batch every 5 minutes    - Progress updates (10%, 20%...)    - Checkpoints saved      LOW: Daily digest    - Completed projects summary    - Cost reports
8. Multi-Modal Input/Output
Input Support:
🔤 Text (natural language, commands)
📎 Files (upload για analysis)
🖼️ Images (screenshots για OCR/Computer Vision)
🔗 URLs (drag & drop)
🎤 Voice (transcribed to text)
Output Formats:
📊 Charts/Graphs (PNG/SVG)
📄 Documents (PDF, Word)
📋 Structured data (JSON, CSV)
🖼️ Screenshots (από browser automation)
🎬 Videos (screen recordings των actions)
9. Conversation Memory
Memory Layers:  Short-term (Session):    - Current project context    - Last 10 messages    - Pending actions      Medium-term (User Profile):    - Preferences (always use PDF, prefer Python)    - Common patterns (συνήθως αναλύει sales data)    - API keys/settings      Long-term (Knowledge):    - Προηγούμενα projects του χρήστη    - Learned patterns από επιτυχημένα tasks    - Custom tool definitions
10. Error Communication Strategy
Level 1 - User Friendly:  ❌ "The website couldn't be reached. Retrying..."Level 2 - Technical Detail (on demand):  📄 Error: ConnectionTimeout (30s)  📄 Stack trace: [View Details]Level 3 - Recovery Options:  🔧 1. Retry with proxy  🔧 2. Use cached version  🔧 3. Skip this step

---# 📄 FILE 45: `application/services/conversation_manager.py````python"""Conversation State Machine για διαχείριση διαλόγου.Handles context switching, multi-turn interactions, memory."""from __future__ import annotationsfrom enum import Enum, autofrom typing import Dict, Optional, List, Any, Callablefrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom datetime import datetime, timedeltaimport asyncioimport structlogimport jsonlogger = structlog.get_logger()class ConversationMode(Enum):    COMMAND = auto()      # One-shot commands    INTERACTIVE = auto()  # Multi-turn dialogue    SUPERVISED = auto()   # Human-in-the-loop (approvals needed)    AUTONOMOUS = auto()   # Background execution, periodic updates@dataclassclass ConversationContext:    """Κατάσταση συνομιλίας."""    session_id: str    user_id: str    mode: ConversationMode = ConversationMode.COMMAND    current_project_id: Optional[str] = None    pending_questions: List[Dict] = field(default_factory=list)    history: List[Dict] = field(default_factory=list)  # Last 20 messages    last_activity: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)    preferences: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)        def touch(self):        self.last_activity = datetime.now()        def is_expired(self, timeout_minutes: int = 30) -> bool:        return datetime.now() - self.last_activity > timedelta(minutes=timeout_minutes)class ConversationManager:    """    Central conversation orchestrator.    """        def __init__(self, project_manager, notification_service):        self.pm = project_manager        self.notifier = notification_service        self.sessions: Dict[str, ConversationContext] = {}        self._response_handlers: Dict[str, Callable] = {}                # Cleanup task        asyncio.create_task(self._cleanup_expired())        async def handle_incoming(        self,        user_id: str,        message: str,        channel: str,        attachments: Optional[List] = None    ) -> str:        """        Main entry point για όλα τα incoming messages.        """        session = self._get_or_create_session(user_id)        session.touch()                # Parse intent        intent = self._parse_intent(message)                # Route based on mode και intent        if session.mode == ConversationMode.SUPERVISED and session.pending_questions:            # User απαντάει σε εκκρεμές ερώτημα            return await self._handle_pending_response(session, message)                if intent["type"] == "command":            return await self._handle_command(session, intent, channel)                if intent["type"] == "natural_language":            return await self._handle_conversational(session, message, channel)                if intent["type"] == "approval":            return await self._handle_approval(session, message)                return "I didn't understand. Try /help"        def _parse_intent(self, message: str) -> Dict:        """Κατανόηση πρόθεσης."""        msg_lower = message.lower().strip()                # Command detection        if msg_lower.startswith(("/task ", "/project ", "/powershell ", "/browser ")):            return {"type": "command", "raw": message}                # Approval/Rejection keywords        if any(k in msg_lower for k in ["approve", "yes", "ok", "confirm"]):            return {"type": "approval", "decision": True}                if any(k in msg_lower for k in ["reject", "no", "cancel", "stop"]):            return {"type": "approval", "decision": False}                # Question answering (numbers, selections)        if msg_lower.isdigit() or msg_lower.startswith(("option ", "choice ")):            return {"type": "selection", "value": msg_lower}                return {"type": "natural_language"}        async def _handle_command(self, session: ConversationContext, intent: Dict, channel: str):        """Χειρισμός εντολών."""        # Transition to interactive για νέο project        session.mode = ConversationMode.INTERACTIVE                # Create project        project = await self.pm.create_project(            user_id=session.user_id,            request=intent["raw"],            channels={channel: channel}        )                session.current_project_id = project.project_id                return f"🎯 Project `{project.project_id}` created.\nAnalyzing requirements..."        async def _handle_conversational(self, session: ConversationContext, message: str, channel: str):        """Φυσικός διάλογος - ρωτάει clarifications."""        if not session.current_project_id:            return "Start with /task <description> or what would you like me to do?"                # Check if we have pending proposals        project = await self.pm.load_project(session.current_project_id)        if project and project.status.name == "PROPOSED":            # User απαντάει σε proposals            return await self.pm.handle_user_response(project.project_id, message)                # General conversation - use LLM για απάντηση        return await self._generate_conversational_response(session, message)        async def ask_user(        self,        session_id: str,        question: str,        options: Optional[List[str]] = None,        timeout_seconds: int = 300,        critical: bool = False    ) -> str:        """        Ρωτάει τον χρήστη και περιμένει απάντηση (blocking με timeout).        """        session = self.sessions.get(session_id)        if not session:            raise ValueError("Session not found")                # Store pending question        question_id = f"q_{datetime.now().timestamp()}"        future = asyncio.get_event_loop().create_future()                self._response_handlers[question_id] = future                session.pending_questions.append({            "id": question_id,            "question": question,            "options": options,            "timestamp": datetime.now(),            "critical": critical        })                session.mode = ConversationMode.SUPERVISED                # Send via notification service        await self.notifier.notify(            severity="CRITICAL" if critical else "INFO",            title="Input Required",            message=question,            metadata={"options": options, "question_id": question_id}        )                # Wait for response        try:            response = await asyncio.wait_for(future, timeout=timeout_seconds)            return response        except asyncio.TimeoutError:            return "TIMEOUT"        def provide_answer(self, question_id: str, answer: str):        """Καλείται όταν ο χρήστης απαντάει."""        if question_id in self._response_handlers:            self._response_handlers[question_id].set_result(answer)            del self._response_handlers[question_id]        async def _cleanup_expired(self):        """Καθαρισμός παλιών sessions."""        while True:            await asyncio.sleep(300)  # Κάθε 5 λεπτά            expired = [                sid for sid, sess in self.sessions.items()                 if sess.is_expired(timeout_minutes=60)            ]            for sid in expired:                del self.sessions[sid]                logger.info("session_expired", session_id=sid)        def _get_or_create_session(self, user_id: str) -> ConversationContext:        if user_id not in self.sessions:            self.sessions[user_id] = ConversationContext(                session_id=f"sess_{user_id}_{datetime.now().timestamp()}",                user_id=user_id            )        return self.sessions[user_id]
Αυτό το σύστημα επιτρέπει φυσική επικοινωνία που προσαρμόζεται στον ρυθμό του χρήστη, με ασύγχρονες δυνατότητες για μακροχρόνιες εργασίες και real-time αλληλεπίδραση όταν χρειάζεται.

# 🤖 Manus-Win11 Enterprise Framework[![Python 3.11+](https://img.shields.io/badge/python-3.11+-blue.svg)](https://www.python.org/downloads/)[![License: MIT](https://img.shields.io/badge/License-MIT-yellow.svg)](https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT)[![Code style: black](https://img.shields.io/badge/code%20style-black-000000.svg)](https://github.com/psf/black)**Production-grade AI agent framework for Windows 11 automation with multi-modal capabilities.**## 🌟 Features- **🧠 Multi-Provider LLM**: Intelligent routing across OpenAI, Claude, Gemini, Kimi (Moonshot), DeepSeek, Qwen, and MiniMax- **🌐 Browser Automation**: Playwright, Puppeteer, and Selenium with connection pooling- **🔍 Advanced Scraping**: Optimized static (BeautifulSoup) and dynamic (Playwright) scraping with automatic strategy selection- **💾 Resumable Projects**: Automatic checkpointing and recovery for long-running tasks- **🗣️ Multi-Platform**: Telegram and Slack integration with rich interactions- **🔒 Enterprise Security**: Capability-based sandboxing, Windows Job Objects, and audit trails- **☁️ Cloud-Native**: Kafka event bus, horizontal scaling, Kubernetes deployment## 🚀 Quick Start### Installation```bash# Clone repositorygit clone https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/manus-win11.gitcd manus-win11# Create virtual environmentpython -m venv venvsource venv/bin/activate  # Windows: venv\Scripts\activate# Install dependenciespip install -r requirements.txt# Install browser dependenciesplaywright install# Configure environmentcp .env.example .env# Edit .env with your API keys
Usage
import asynciofrom manus_win11 import ManusEngine, Configasync def main():    config = Config.from_yaml("config.yaml")        async with ManusEngine(config) as engine:        # Simple task        result = await engine.execute(            tool="powershell",            command="Get-Process | Select-Object -First 5"        )        print(result.output)        # Autonomous project with enhancements        project = await engine.create_project(            "Analyze sales data and create quarterly report"        )        # Agent will propose enhancements, wait for approval, then executeif __name__ == "__main__":    asyncio.run(main())

#!/bin/bash# 1. Μπες στον φάκελο του projectcd ~/manus-win11  # ή όπου είναι τα αρχεία σου# 2. Αρχικοποίηση Git (αν δεν έχεις κάνει ήδη)git init# 3. Πρόσθεσε όλα τα αρχείαgit add .# 4. Commitgit commit -m "feat: Initial commit - Manus-Win11 Enterprise FrameworkComplete AI agent framework featuring:- Multi-provider LLM routing (OpenAI, Claude, Gemini, Kimi, DeepSeek, Qwen, MiniMax)- Browser automation (Playwright, Puppeteer, Selenium)- Advanced scraping (BeautifulSoup, Scrapy)- Distributed event-driven architecture with Kafka- Resumable projects with checkpointing- Vector database integration (ChromaDB)- Telegram & Slack bot integration- Kubernetes deployment ready- Safety sandboxing with Windows Job Objects"# 5. Σύνδεση με το GitHub repo σουgit remote add origin https://github.com/georgehadji/weebot.git# 6. Ορισμός main branchgit branch -M main# 7. Push!git push -u origin main
📋 Βήμα-Βήμα (Αν δεν έχεις φτιάξει τα αρχεία ακόμα)
Πρώτα φτιάξε το project:
# Δημιούργησε φάκελοmkdir ~/weebotcd ~/weebot# Δημιούργησε τη δομήmkdir -p {domain,application/services,infrastructure/{llm,browser,scraping,messaging,heartbeat,comms,vector_db,plugins},deployment/{docker,k8s},tests,docs}# Δημιούργησε τα βασικά αρχεία (αντιγράφοντας τον κώδικα από πάνω)# ...
Μετά κάνε push:
git initgit add .git commit -m "Initial commit"git remote add origin https://github.com/georgehadji/weebot.gitgit branch -M maingit push -u origin main
🔐 Πριν το Push - Έλεγξε:
Έχεις κάνει create το repo στο GitHub;→ Πήγαινε στο https://github.com/new και φτιάξε ένα κενό repo με όνομα weebot
Έχεις configure τα credentials;
git config --global user.name "George Hadji"git config --global user.email "your-email@example.com"
Αν σου ζητήσει password στο push, χρησιμοποίησε Personal Access Token (όχι το κανονικό σου password):
https://github.com/settings/tokens
Δημιούργησε token με δικαιώματα repo
Χρησιμοποίησε αυτό ως password
✅ Επιβεβαίωση μετά το Push
# Έλεγξε ότι έγινε σωστάgit status# Θα πρέπει να δεις: "On branch main, Your branch is up to date with 'origin/main'"# Δες το loggit log --oneline
Μετά άνοιξε το https://github.com/georgehadji/weebot και θα δεις τον κώδικά σου online!
Θες να σου γράψω συγκεκριμένα το περιεχόμενο των αρχείων (domain/entities.py, infrastructure/llm/router.py, κλπ) για να τα αποθηκεύσεις πριν κάνεις το push;
